	<h1 class="firstHeading" id="firstHeading" lang="en">EuroBasket Women 2015 squads</h1>
	
	<div class="mw-body-content" id="bodyContent">
		<div class="noprint" id="siteSub">From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia</div>
		<div id="contentSub"></div>
		
		
		
		<div id="jump-to-nav"></div>

		<div class="mw-content-ltr" dir="ltr" id="mw-content-text" lang="en"><div class="mw-parser-output"><div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/EuroBasket_Women_2015" title="EuroBasket Women 2015">EuroBasket Women 2015</a></div>
<p>This article displays the rosters for the teams competing at the <a href="/wiki/EuroBasket_Women_2015" title="EuroBasket Women 2015">EuroBasket Women 2015</a>. Each team has to submit 12 players.
</p>
